    13	#include <unordered_map>
    14	
    15	#ifndef CHAISCRIPT_NO_THREADS
    16	#include <mutex>
    17	#include <shared_mutex>
    18	#include <thread>
    19	#else
    20	#ifndef CHAISCRIPT_NO_THREADS_WARNING
    21	#pragma message("ChaiScript is compiling without thread safety.")
    22	#endif
    23	#endif
    24	
    25	#include "chaiscript_defines.hpp"
    26	
    27	/// \file
    28	///
    29	/// This file contains code necessary for thread support in ChaiScript.
    30	/// If the compiler definition CHAISCRIPT_NO_THREADS is defined then thread safety
    31	/// is disabled in ChaiScript. This has the result that some code is faster, because mutex locks are not required.
    32	/// It also has the side effect that the chaiscript::ChaiScript object may not be accessed from more than
    33	/// one thread simultaneously.
    34	
    35	/// If threading is enabled, then this namespace contains std thread classes.
    36	/// If threading is not enabled, then stubbed in wrappers that do nothing are provided.
    37	/// This allows us to avoid \#ifdef code in the sections that need thread safety.
    38	namespace chaiscript::detail::threading {
    39	#ifndef CHAISCRIPT_NO_THREADS
    40	
    41	  template<typename T>
    42	  using unique_lock = std::unique_lock<T>;
    43	
    44	  template<typename T>
    45	  using shared_lock = std::shared_lock<T>;
    46	
    47	  template<typename T>
    48	  using lock_guard = std::lock_guard<T>;
    49	
    50	  using std::shared_mutex;
    51	
    52	  using std::mutex;
    53	
    54	  using std::recursive_mutex;
    55	
    56	  /// Typesafe thread specific storage. If threading is enabled, this class uses a mutex protected map. If
    57	  /// threading is not enabled, the class always returns the same data, regardless of which thread it is called from.
    58	  template<typename T>
    59	  class Thread_Storage {
    60	  public:
    61	    Thread_Storage() = default;
    62	    Thread_Storage(const Thread_Storage &) = delete;
    63	    Thread_Storage(Thread_Storage &&) = delete;
    64	    Thread_Storage &operator=(const Thread_Storage &) = delete;
    65	    Thread_Storage &operator=(Thread_Storage &&) = delete;
    66	
    67	    ~Thread_Storage() { t().erase(this); }
    68	
    69	    inline const T *operator->() const noexcept { return &(t()[this]); }
    70	
    71	    inline const T &operator*() const noexcept { return t()[this]; }
    72	
    73	    inline T *operator->() noexcept { return &(t()[this]); }
    74	
    75	    inline T &operator*() noexcept { return t()[this]; }
    76	
    77	    void *m_key;
    78	
    79	  private:
    80	    /// todo: is it valid to make this noexcept? The allocation could fail, but if it
    81	    /// does there is no possible way to recover
    82	    static std::unordered_map<const void *, T> &t() noexcept {
    83	      static thread_local std::unordered_map<const void *, T> my_t;
    84	      return my_t;
    85	    }
    86	  };
    87	
    88	#else // threading disabled
    89	  template<typename T>
    90	  class unique_lock {
    91	  public:
    92	    constexpr explicit unique_lock(T &) noexcept {}
    93	    constexpr void lock() noexcept {}
    94	    constexpr void unlock() noexcept {}
    95	  };
    96	
    97	  template<typename T>
    98	  class shared_lock {
    99	  public:
   100	    constexpr explicit shared_lock(T &) noexcept {}
   101	    constexpr void lock() noexcept {}
   102	    constexpr void unlock() noexcept {}
   103	  };
   104	
   105	  template<typename T>
   106	  class lock_guard {
   107	  public:
   108	    constexpr explicit lock_guard(T &) noexcept {}
   109	  };
   110	
   111	  class shared_mutex {
   112	  };
   113	
   114	  class recursive_mutex {
   115	  };
   116	
   117	  template<typename T>
   118	  class Thread_Storage {
   119	  public:
   120	    constexpr explicit Thread_Storage() noexcept {}
   121	
   122	    constexpr inline T *operator->() const noexcept { return &obj; }
   123	
   124	    constexpr inline T &operator*() const noexcept { return obj; }
   125	
   126	  private:
   127	    mutable T obj;
   128	  };
   129	
   130	#endif
   131	} // namespace chaiscript::detail::threading

   128	    for (const auto c : t_str) {
   129	      if (c < '0' || c > '9') {

🎬 ACTION
cat > /tmp/repro_tsan_threads.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed

workflow=.github/workflows/ci.yml

# Every TSAN CMake configure command must explicitly enable ChaiScript threading.
tsancmds=$(grep -n 'ENABLE_THREAD_SANITIZER=ON' "$workflow" || true)
if [[ -z "$tsancmds" ]]; then
  echo "No TSAN configure commands found" >&2
  exit 1
fi
if echo "$tsancmds" | grep -v 'MULTITHREAD_SUPPORT_ENABLED=ON' >/dev/null; then
  echo "TSAN configure command(s) do not explicitly enable threading:" >&2
  echo "$tsancmds" | grep -v 'MULTITHREAD_SUPPORT_ENABLED=ON' >&2
  exit 1
fi

# At least one Windows/MSVC CMake configure command must explicitly enable ChaiScript threading.
python3 - <<'PY'
from pathlib import Path
text = Path('.github/workflows/ci.yml').read_text().splitlines()
in_windows = False
found = False
for line in text:
    if line.startswith('  ') and not line.startswith('    ') and line.strip().endswith(':'):
        in_windows = line.strip() == 'windows:'
    if in_windows and 'run: cmake' in line and 'MULTITHREAD_SUPPORT_ENABLED=ON' in line:
        found = True
if not found:
    raise SystemExit('No Windows/MSVC configure command explicitly enables threading')
PY
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_tsan_threads.sh
/tmp/repro_tsan_threads.sh

rm -rf /tmp/chai-tsan-config-check /tmp/chai-nothreads-config-check
cmake -S /testbed -B /tmp/chai-tsan-config-check -DENABLE_THREAD_SANITIZER=ON -DMULTITHREAD_SUPPORT_ENABLED=OFF -DBUILD_TESTING=OFF >/tmp/chai-tsan-config.log
if ! grep -Eq 'MULTITHREAD_SUPPORT_ENABLED:BOOL=(ON|TRUE)' /tmp/chai-tsan-config-check/CMakeCache.txt; then
  echo 'TSAN did not force threading on'
  grep 'MULTITHREAD_SUPPORT_ENABLED' /tmp/chai-tsan-config-check/CMakeCache.txt || true
  exit 1
fi
cmake -S /testbed -B /tmp/chai-nothreads-config-check -DMULTITHREAD_SUPPORT_ENABLED=OFF -DBUILD_TESTING=OFF >/tmp/chai-nothreads-config.log
if ! grep -q 'MULTITHREAD_SUPPORT_ENABLED:BOOL=OFF' /tmp/chai-nothreads-config-check/CMakeCache.txt; then
  echo 'Explicit non-TSAN no-thread configure was not preserved'
  grep 'MULTITHREAD_SUPPORT_ENABLED' /tmp/chai-nothreads-config-check/CMakeCache.txt || true
  exit 1
fi
echo 'final checks passed'
